Et s’il ne revient en ceste maniere, si covient que tu apareilles I ministre fort, et esten la jambe fort a II mains, ou a I liien que soit liiez sus lou genoil; et uns autres ministres estende sa main desus en teil maniere qu’il boute ses mains desoz ses asseles, puis l’estrigne d’un souef liien sus la cuixe; et uns autres tigne lou chief dou liien; et estendent amont et aval tuit a une fois, tant que li malaide soit levez de terre a une fois, et demoure pendans.	 And if it does not return in this manner, then you must call for a strong assistant, and stretch the leg strongly with two hands, or with one rope tied above the knee; and another assistant stretches his hand on top in such a way that he pushes his hands under his buttocks, then pulls with a soft rope above the thigh; and another holds the end of the rope; and they all pull up and down at once, until the patient is lifted off the ground at once, and remains hanging.
Ceste maniere d’estension si est commune as IIII semblances, et se li dislocation est revenue, si com nos avons dit, c’est bien.	 This manner of extension is common to four resemblances, and if the dislocation returns, as we have said, it is good.
Se ceu non, si covient mettre cure a sa semblance Quant li dislocations est au pardedens, si covient que tu sovines le malaide sus son costeit sain, puis met le liien sus la racine de la cuixe, et le leu qui est desoz l’angre, puis estent le liien en haut devers l’angre, et devers la forcele; puis preigne uns autres ministres ses bras, et embraice le gros leu de la cuixe malaide, et l’estende au defuer forment: si revenra a son leu maintenant; et ceste maniere de dislocation est plus legiere des autres.	 If not, then one must apply care to its resemblance. When the dislocation is in the hip, it is necessary that you place the patient on his healthy side, then put the bandage on the root of the thigh, and the place under the buttock, then extend the bandage upward toward the buttock and toward the groin; then let another minister take his arms, and embrace the thick part of the unhealthy thigh, and stretch it very firmly: it will return to its place now; and this manner of dislocation is lighter than others.
Et se tu ne la pues serrer en ceste maniere que nos avons dit, si covient que tu lies les II piés dou malaide ensamble d’un fort liien souef sus les II talons, et sus les II genous, et soit li jambe malaide estendue II dois plus que li autres; puis soit pendus sus le chief d’un fust, et soit en sus de terre II bras de lonc; puis comande a I ministre qu’il embraice le chief de la cuixe, et soit uns autres ministres pendans avec le malaide, qui embraice forment la cuixe, car li jointure revient maintenant hastanment.	 And if you cannot secure it in the manner we have described, then you must bind together the two feet of the patient with a strong and soft ligature at the level of the two ankles, and the two knees; and let the afflicted leg be extended two fingers' width more than the other. Then hang it from the top of a pole, and let there be two arms' length between it and the ground. Then instruct one assistant to embrace the thigh just above the knee, and let another assistant hanging with the patient strongly embrace the thigh, for the joint now returns quickly.
Et quant li dislocations est au defuer, si gise li malaides, si com nos avons dit en celui qui a gilbositeit, et estraigne I liien sus la jambe malaide proprement, et sus le peis ausi; puis met II tisons, I au chief et I autre as piez, puis fiche I tison entre les cuixes au malaide emmi la forme; et ait plantei de drapelz moistes entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide, puis estende chescuns ministre devers lui, et li mires mette igal a sa main la dislocation.	 And when the dislocation is out, let the patient lie down as we have said for one with gout, and tighten the ligature on the afflicted leg and also on the foot; then place two splints, one at the head and the other at the feet, then insert a splint between the thighs of the patient in this manner. And let moist cloths be placed around so that it does not injure the patient. Then let each assistant stretch towards him, and the physician set the dislocation level with his hand.
S’elle revient, c’est boin.	 S’elle revient, c’est boin.
Se ce non, met sus .ie. table, et le presse ensi com nos avons dit en la gilbositeit, et gise li malaides sus le sain costeit.	 If not, place the patient on a table and press as we have said in the case of dislocation, and let the patient lie on their sound side.
Et quant li dislocations est devant, si covient estendre la jambe malaide hastanment, et selonc ce que j’ai dit; et mette li mires sa paine d’estre sus l’angre malaide, puis presse a l’autre main, et l’estent aval devers lou genoil.	 And when the dislocation is forward, it is necessary to quickly extend the affected leg according to what I have said; and let the physician place his weight on the affected ankle, then press with the other hand, and stretch downwards towards the knee.
Et se li dislocations est au defuer, si ne covient pas estendre le malaide aval, ne lever sus la terre, ains covient qu’il soit ausi com se li hainche estoit desaluee au defuer, si com nos avons dit dou couchement sus les II hainches; et soit sus sa faice, et li lien estendut si com nos avons dit ci devant, et doit om presser sus la jointure a la table; et sera a point quant li malaides estendra ses jambes, et elles seront igalz; adonques ajoste les cuixes, et met l’emplaustre, et l’estrain d’un bendeil, si que li hainche ne se mueve; et se repose III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie, et met l’emplaustre sus; et se tu vois qu’elles soient igalz, si l’estrain, si com devant, et le laisse III jors; puis le deslie, et lou fai aler belement, tant que li membres soit confortez.	 And if the dislocation is backward, it is not necessary to extend the affected limb downwards or lift it off the ground, but it should be as if the hip were dislocated backward, as we have said about lying on both hips; and let him lie on his face, with the ligaments stretched as we have said before, and someone should press on the joint against the table; and it will be ready when the patient extends his legs and they are equal; then bring the thighs together, and apply the poultice, and bind tightly with a bandage so that the hip does not move; and let him rest for three days or four, then unbind, and apply the poultice again; and if you see that they are equal, then bind as before, and leave it for three days; then unbind, and let him walk well until the limb is healed.  /> And if the dislocation is backward, it is not necessary to extend the affected limb downwards or lift it off the ground, but it should be as if the hip were dislocated backward, as we have said about lying on both hips; and let him lie on his face, with the ligaments stretched as we have said before, and someone should press on the joint against the table; and it will be ready when the patient extends his legs and they are equal; then bring the thighs together, and apply the poultice, and bind tightly with a bandage so that the hip does not move; and let him rest for three days or four, then unbind, and apply the poultice again; and if you see that they are equal, then bind as before, and leave it for three days; then unbind, and let him walk well until the limb is healed.  /> And if the dislocation is backward, it is not necessary to extend the affected limb downwards or lift it off the ground, but it should be as if the hip were dislocated backward, as we have said about lying on both hips; and let him lie on his face, with the ligaments stretched as we have said before, and someone should press on the joint against the table; and it will be ready when the patient extends his legs and they are equal; and if you see that they are equal, then bind as before, and leave it for three days; then unbind, and let him walk well until the limb is healed.
de la dislocation dou genoil	 of the knee dislocation
Li genous est desaluez selonc III manieres: c’est a savoir, dedens et defuer, et derrier; et ne desalue point devant.	 The knee is dislocated in three ways: that is to say, inside and outside, and behind; and does not dislocate in front.
Et li signes si est que tu comande au malaide qu’il plie sa jambe a sa cuixe, et s’ele ne s’aert a sa cuixe, saiches qu’il est desaluez; et li restauration de toutes si est que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et estende sa jambe s’il puet, et li met ton dos sus sa faice, et met son piet sus tes piez; puis pren son genoil a tes paumes, et retrai entre tes dois, puis plie les II costez dou genoil forment; et uns autres ministres estende son piet, tant que li genous reviegne a son leu, et li signes est qu’il aert bien sa jambe a sa cuixe legierement; et met l’emplastre sus, et fai aerdre la jambe a la cuixe, et les loie ensamble fort III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie; et ne se travaille mie li malaides d’aler, tant que li membres soit confortez.	 And the sign is that you instruct the patient to bend his leg to his thigh, and if it does not reach his thigh, know that it is dislocated; and the restoration of all [three] is that you make the patient sit upright, and extend his leg if he can, and place your back on his face, and put his foot on your feet; then take his knee between your palms, and pull back between your teeth, then strongly bend the two sides of the knee; and another attendant extends his foot, so that the knee returns to its place, and the sign is that he easily bends his leg to his thigh; and put the bandage on, and make the leg adhere to the thigh, and bind them together strongly for three days or four, then unbind; and the patient should not attempt to walk until the limb is healed.
Et se li membres n’est a point, si aministre estendement fort, si com nos avons dit en la cure de la hainche, tant qu’il soit sanez	 And if the limb is not at all, administer strong extension, as we have said in the treatment of the hip, until it is healed.
de la dislocation dou talon	 of the ankle dislocation
Li talons est aucune fois esmeus, et aucune fois desaluez plenement, et dedens et defuer.	 The ankles are sometimes swollen and sometimes fully dislocated, both inside and out.
Et li signes si est que li cheville est enflee, et tent avant a la partie ou elle est desaluee: li ramenemens si est legier, et le doit on estendre legierement a ses mains quant il est esmeus soulement.	 And the sign of this is that the ankle is swollen and extends forward to the part where it is dislocated; the reduction should be gentle, and one should extend it gently with their hands when it is only swollen.
Et quant il est desaluez dou tot, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et le tigne I ministres fors par la jambe, desus la cheville; puis trai le piet a toi a ta main destre, et puis a la senestre II fois, puis l’estent en haut, et boute bellement lou piet en haut; et fai ce II fois, si com nos avons dit, em boutant et en traiant lou piet; s’elle revient, c’est bien; se ce non, si rencomence l’ovraige, car il revient; et s’il ne puet revenir ensi, si fai gesir lou malaide sor son dos sus terre, et fiche I passeil fermement en terre entre ses cuixes, et lie drapelz entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide; puis teigne li ministres la cuixe, et uns autres ministres estende lou piet a ses mains ou a I liien, k’il lie sus le col dou piet; puis estende chescuns ministres igalment, et li passelz soit adés entre les cuixes dou malaide por retenir le malaide quant on l’estent; puis mette li mires igal la dislocation a ses mains, et uns autres ministres teigne la jambe sainne au desoz, et li dislocation revenra hastanment.	 And when it is fully dislocated, one should make the patient sit upright, and have two assistants hold the leg above the ankle; then pull the foot towards yourself with your right hand, and then with your left hand twice, then extend it upwards, and push the foot nicely upwards; and do this twice, as we have said, by pushing and pulling the foot; if it returns, that's good; if not, begin the work again, for it will return; and if it cannot return thus, make the patient lie on their back on the ground, and drive a firm stake into the ground between their thighs, and tie cloths around, so that they do not hurt the patient; then let one assistant hold the thigh, and another extend the foot in their hands or with a rope tied above the ankle; then extend each assistant equally, and the stake should be always between the patient's thighs to support the patient when extending; then let the doctor place the dislocation evenly in their hands, and another assistant hold the healthy leg below, and the dislocation will quickly return.
Et quant elle iert a point, si met l’emplastre et estoupes sus, et l’estrain forment, et lie lou piet a la jambe, et warde les ners qui sont sus la cheville derrier, que li liiens ne soit trop estrois; puis le laisse II jors ou III, et se li liiens amolist, si l’estrain; puis le deslie au tier jor ou au quart, et deffent a aler lou malaide par IIII jors; et s’il va devant cel termine, ce n’est mie seurtez qu’il ne desalue encor.	 And when it is fully healed, apply the bandage and wool on top, and bind tightly, and tie the foot to the leg, and protect the nerves that are above the ankle in the back, so that the binding is not too tight; then leave it for two or three days, and if the binding loosens, rebind it; then remove it on the third day or the fourth, and forbid the patient from walking for four days; and if he goes before this time, it is not safe that he will not dislocate again.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si covient que tu l’apaises, si com nos avons dit autre part, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And if such abscesses occur, it is necessary that you treat them, as we have said elsewhere, until they are healed.
des dois	 of the two
Quant li doi sont desaluez, si les covient bellement estendre sens travail, et c’est legiere chose.	 When the fingers are dislocated, they must be carefully extended without effort, and this is a simple matter.
Et se li dislocations est en aucun nout dou dos dou piet, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide sus I leu plain ou sus .ie. table tot droit, et met ton piet sus ce qui apert de ces jointures, puis presse a ton piet forment, tant qu’il reviegne; et quant il est igalz, et il n’i apert nient, si met desoz la plante dou piet une table a II chiés, puis l’estrain forment, et le laisse III jors, puis le deslie; et le fai reposer, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And if the dislocation is in any joint of the foot, then you must make the patient sit or lie flat on a table, and place your foot over the prominent part of these joints, then press firmly with your foot until it returns; and when it is aligned, and nothing protrudes, place a two-legged table under the sole of the foot, then tighten it firmly and leave it for three days, then remove it; and let it rest until it heals.
de plaie et de dislocation ensamble	 of wounds and dislocations together
Quant plaie vient avec la dislocation, et on la vuet restorer, maintes fois avient que li malaides muert: si ne soies mie presumptuous en la cure, se tu n’es saiges en l’art et tu ne l’as useit longement, et se tu n’es pitous et misericors et tardis, ne mie hardis; et use au comencement de choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et laisse le malaide en la main Deu, se tu n’i vois esperance de santeit; et quant tu i vois esperance, si ramoinne maintenant le membre au leu, ainsois que li apostemes chaus i viegne; et quant li membres est a leu, si aministre choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et cure la plaie, si com il covient, d’oignemens desiccatis; et se avec la dislocation a brisure, et os menus desevrez, si les oste, et fai ce que nos avons dit en maladies simples; et te garde d’entrer en voie de paour, selonc ce que j’ai dit, car ce te vaut mues selonc ton Creator, et por la saveteit de t’arme et de ton cors.	 When a wound comes with dislocation and you want to restore it, it often happens that the patient dies: so do not be presumptuous in the cure if you are not wise in the art and have not practiced it for a long time, and if you are not merciful and patient and cautious, not bold; and at first use things that calm down inflammation, and leave the patient in God's hands if you do not see hope of health; and when you see hope, then reset the limb before the inflammation comes; and when the limb is in place, administer things that calm down inflammation, and treat the wound with desiccating ointments as needed; and if there is a fracture with dislocation and small bones are broken, remove them, and do what we have said in simple diseases; and beware of entering into fear, according to what I have said, for this is worthless according to your Creator, and for the wisdom of your weapon and your body.
Amen	 Amen
